follows a two-stage model: static registration at initialization and per-connection instantiation at runtime.\\n\\n### 1. Filter Factory Registry and Registration\\n\\n**Core Interface** (envoy/server/filter_config.h):\\n- `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Base interface for HTTP filter factories. Each HTTP filter implements a config factory that extends this interface.\\n- `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Parallel interface for upstream-specific HTTP filters.\\n\\nFilters are registered statically using `Registry::RegisterFactory<FilterConfigType, NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>()`. The registry (Registry::FactoryRegistry<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>) stores factories indexed by their type name.\\n\\n### 2. Factory Callback and Filter Instantiation\\n\\n**Core Types** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):\\n- `FilterFactoryCb` - Function type `std::function<void(FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&)>` that creates and installs filters for a stream. Factories return this callback during initialization.\\n- `FilterChainManager` - Abstract interface with `applyFilterFactoryCb()` method, implemented per-connection to manage filter instantiation.\\n- `FilterChainFactory` - Interface for creating filter chains, with `createFilterChain()` called when new streams arrive.\\n\\n### 3. Configuration and Filter Chain Creation\\n\\n**Configuration Processing** (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h and config.cc):\\n- `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` implements `Http::FilterChainFactory`.\\n- During construction, it uses `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()` (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h) to process the HTTP filters configuration.\\n- `processFilters()` iterates through each filter in the config and:\\n  - Retrieves the factory from the registry using `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<>`\\n  - Creates a `FilterConfigProvider` using `filter_config_provider_manager_.createStaticFilterConfigProvider()`\\n  - For dynamic filters, creates `HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl` (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h) which manages runtime filter config updates\\n\\n**Key Data Structure** (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h line 185-189):\\n```cpp\\nstruct NamedHttpFilterFactoryCb {\\n  std::string name;                    // Canonical filter name\\n  Http::FilterFactoryCb factory_cb;   // Factory function\\n};\\n```\\n\\n### 4. Dynamic Filter Configuration\\n\\n**Runtime Updates** (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h line 195-229):\\n- `HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl` manages filters that can be updated at runtime via xDS.\\n- When a config update arrives, `instantiateFilterFactory()` is called (line 221-229):\\n  - follows a two-stage model: static registration at initialization and per-connection instantiation at runtime.\\n\\n### 1. Filter Factory Registry and Registration\\n\\n**Core Interface** (envoy/server/filter_config.h):\\n- `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Base interface for HTTP filter factories. Each HTTP filter implements a config factory that extends this interface.\\n- `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Parallel interface for upstream-specific HTTP filters.\\n\\nFilters are registered statically using `Registry::RegisterFactory<FilterConfigType, NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>()`. Factories return this callback during initialization.\\n- `FilterChainManager` - Abstract interface with `applyFilterFactoryCb()` method, implemented per-connection to manage filter instantiation.\\n- `FilterChainFactory` - Interface for creating filter chains, with `createFilterChain()` called when new streams arrive.\\n\\n### 3.
